Dialog VENDOR
'-----PROGRAM CHOOSES AN EX°CEL WORKSHEET BASED ON VENDOR----------------------­
If VENDOR.SELECT = Then
GALVENIZE = MsgBox ("Will the parts be Galvanized?", 4, "GALVANIZING")
If GALVENIZE = 6 Then
COSTSHEET = "HPM"
Else
COSTSHEET = "HPMNon"
MsgBox "This program does not handle non-galvanized assemblies for HPM. See the program administrator. ",0
Exit Sub
End If
Elseif VENDOR.SELECT = 1 Then
COSTSHEET = "PREMIER"
PROJECT = InputBox$ ("Enter the project number.",,)
Elseif VENDOR. SELECT = 2 Then
COSTSHEET = "MARKLE"
PROJECT = InputBox$ ("Enter the project number.",,)
Else
COSTSHEET = "OTHER"
PROJECT = InputBox$ (" Enter the proj ect number.",,)
End If
'-----IF NOT HPM, PROGRAM CHECKS PRICING SETUP--------------------------------­
'--------IF PROJECT PRICING HAS NOT BE SET IN EXCEL, THE PROGRAM WILL BE------­
,--------TERMINATED.----------------------------------------------------------­
Set Excel = CreateObject ("Excel.Application")
Excel.Workbooks.Open FileName:= "\\HPC_HOUSTON\VOL2\PRODUCTS\TRANSFERFOLDER\DRAFTING\Sublets\OUtside Subcontract Pricing.xls"
If COSTSHEET = "PREMIER" Then
Excel.Worksheets("Premier") .Activate
PROJECTTEST = Exce1 . Range ("C2" )
Elseif COSTSHEET = "MARKLE" Then
Excel. Worksheets ("Markle") .Activate
PROJEC'I"I'EST = Excel. Range (" C2")
Elseif COSTSHEET = "OTHER" Then
Excel. Worksheets ("Other") .Activate
PROJEC'I"I'EST = Excel. Range ( "C3")
Else
Excel.Worksheets("HPM") .Activate
Goto Continue2:
End If
If PROJECT = PROJECTTEST Then
Goto Continue2:

Sub Main
Dim SELECTION As Integer
Dim ASSY As String
Dim CR As String '---'CR' IS USED AS A CARRIAGE RETURN-----­
CR = Chr$(rcCR)
'-----USER SELECTS BETWEEN ENTERING WEIGHTS AND COSTS-------------------------­
Begin Dialog TaskRequest 200,64,"PROGRAM TASK"
ButtonGroup.CHOICE
Text 20,10,160,28,"Do you want to enter weights or costs?"
Button 20,46,70,14, "WEIGHTS"
Button 110,46,70,14,"COSTS"
End Dialog
Dim TASK As TaskRequest
Dialog TASK
,-----USER SUPPLIES THE PART NUMBER OF THE SUBCONTRACTED ASSEMBLY-------------­
ASSY = InputBox$ ("Enter the part number of the skeleton-level assembly. Use only uppercase letters.",,)
IF ASSY = "" THEN °
MsgBox "PROGRAM CANCELED",
Exit Sub
End If
'-----MAIN PROGRAM SENDS CONTROL TO APPROPRIATE SUB-PROGRAM-------------------­
If TASK. CHOICE = 1 Then
Call COST (SELECTION), (ASSY), (CR))
Else
Begin Dialog CalcRequest 200,64,"PROGRAM CALCULATIONS"
ButtonGroup.PARTS
Text 20,10,160,28,"For which ETO parts will weights be calculated?"
Button 20,46,70,14,"COMPONENTS"
Button 110,46,70,14,"ASSEMBLIES"
End Dialog
Dim CALC As CalcRequest
Dialog CALC °
If CALC. PARTS = Then
Call WEIGHTCOMP (ASSY, (CR))
Else
Call WEIGHTASSY (ASSY, (CR))
End If
End If
End Sub

I I I I
HUDSON PRODUCTS CORPORATION
STDBOOK SECT.7A-PG.D-l
D ETO PART ENTRY
Purpose & Introduction
This program is designed to enter part numbers into Visibility from a Microsoft Excel template. It
allows the PMA to use some ofthe features ofExcel to build part numbers and descriptions quickly. It
also removes a lot ofthe redundancy in data entry from part number to part number (i.e., various flags)
and removes the error associated with choosing the wrong hot key. While the program can be used for a
variety ofparts, it was designed to be used to enter ETa, manufactured parts (this includes sub­
contracted parts). Using it to enter any other parts may result in errors with running the program or with
the data entered.
Instructions for Use
1 Open MS Excel.
2 From the 'File' menu, select 'New...'.
3 On the 'General' tab, select the template, 'Part Entry', then the 'OK' button.
4 Enter the following data for each part you wish to enter into Visibility. You can use features ofMS
Excel to speed up the input ofthis data (e.g., 'AutoFill', 'Cut-and-Paste', etc.).
4.1 All data entered must be in capital letters. You should press the 'Caps Lock' key before
starting.
4.2 The cursor should be in cell 'A6' ofworksheet 'ETa-Make' when the workbook is started.
4.3 Enter the project number in column A.
4.4 Enter the drawing number in column B.
4.5 Enter the piece mark ofthe part to be entered in column C.
4.6 Enter the start ofthe description into column D, per ETO Part Description Formats in
Engineering Standards Book I, section 4B.
A list ofthese 'Description Nouns' can be found in the worksheet 'Description Lists' in
the active Excel workbook. This list should be maintained by the Standards department.
However, due to the logistics ofupdating the Excel template, it may lag behind the
procedure. This list is intended to be used as an aid to part description look-up. The
standards book will always supercede the list in the Excel template.
4.7 Ifthe description is required to show the width ofthe raw material, enter the elements ofthat
dimension as follows.
4.7.1 inches in column E
4.7.2 numerator ofthe inch fraction (ifany) in column F
4.7.3 denominator ofthe inch fraction (if any) in column G
4.8 Ifthe description is required to show the length ofthe raw material, enter the elements ofthat
dimension as follows.
4.8.1 feet in column H (if less then 1 foot, enter 0)
4.8.2 inches in column I (ifzero inches, enter 0)
4.8.3 numerator ofthe inch fraction (ifany) in column J
4.8.4 denominator ofthe inch fraction (if any) in column K
4.9 Enter the data for the next part into the next row, starting with column A. Remember that
Excel has several tools available to copy data. This is very helpful when entering the project,
drawing number, description noun, etc.
4.10 Enter the number ofthe last Excel row that contains a part number to be entered in cell 'B5'.
AUTOMATION DOCUMENTATION REV. 0, 3-6-00

I I I I
STDBOOK HUDSON PRODUCTS CORPORATION SECT.7A-PG.D-2
4.11 If you are entering part numbers ofassemblies that will be purchased from vendors, you can
switch to the worksheet 'ETO-Sub' at this time.
4.12 Enter these other parts in a similar manner to the 'ETO-Make' parts. The only parts that
should be entered on this worksheet should be the actual part numbers that will appear on the
purchase order and be received either at the HPC-Beasley facility, the job site, or some other
staging location. The difference in procedure for 'ETO-Sub' parts is as follows.
4.12.1 After entering all dimension information (ifrequired), enter the buyer code into
column L.
4.12.2 Enter the cost type ofthe part into column M.
4.12.3 Enter the engineering category into column N.
4.13 Review the description character sets (columns S, U, and W for the 'ETO-Make' worksheet,
and columns U, W, and Y for the 'ETO-Sub' worksheet).
4.13.1 Review the numbers in columns T, V, and X ofworksheet 'ETO-Make' and columns
V, X, and Z ofworksheet 'ETO-Sub'.
4.13.2 These numbers are a count ofthe number ofcharacters in the cell to the left ofthat
column. This number should never exceed 30.
4.13.3 The worksheets are set up so that ifthe first set ofcharacters (columns S for 'make'
parts and U for 'sub' parts) exceeds 30, the description will be broken up between this
first set and the second set (columns U for 'make' parts and W for 'sub' parts).
4.13.4 Ifthe third set ofcharacters (columns W for 'make' parts and Y for 'sub' parts) is
needed or ifthe program doesn't break up the descriptions properly, you will have to
enter the description into the 3 columns manually. Take care not to allow any set of
characters to exceed 30.
5 From the 'File' menu, select 'Save As...' and save the file as 'c:\My Documents\Part Entry.xIs,. If
entering a large number ofparts, you may want to save often, during step 4.
6 Select the worksheet 'ETO-Make'.
7 Using the mouse, select all cells starting from row 6 through the row after the last row in which data
has been entered. You will need to include columns R, S, T, U, V, W, and X in the selection area.
8 From the 'File' menu, select 'Print Area ~ Set Print Area'.
9 Repeat steps 7 and 8 for the worksheet 'ETO-Sub', ifany parts were entered there, with the
exception that columns T, U, V, W, X, Y, and Z should be included in the selection area.
10 Select the printer icon from within each worksheet. This will print your selected print area. If
nothing was entered into 'ETO-Sub', do not select the printer icon from within that worksheet.
11 Submit the printout, with drawings, for checking.
12 After receiving the marked-up copy ofthe printout, make all necessary corrections.
13 Save the file using the save icon.
14 Close MS Excel.
15 Log into Visibility and move the cursor in Visibility to the 'Selection:' field in the 'Main Menu'.
16 From the 'Scril!t' menu, select 'Run Script...'.
17 Select the script 'Part Entry' from within the default Reflection script director on your PC. Then
select the 'Run' button.
18 If the program hangs, encounters any errors during execution, or starts beeping rapidly (but not
necessarily continuously) while entering no data, see the program administrator immediately.
19 The script should leave the cursor back in the 'Selection:' field ofthe 'Main Menu'.
20 When the program has finished, delete the file 'c:\My Documents\Part Entry.xls'. This will help to
avoid your accidentally trying to enter parts more than once.

numbers are as shown below. Deviations should be approved by Production

5.12.4 TOOLING
5.12.4.1 Bundles with thick walled tubes will require the cost ofrolling be
included. This cost is to be entered into the HOOO-6X-3 BOM using
the part number TOOLING with a quantity equal to the total cost for
all tubes in the bundle.
5.12.4.2 Use tables 3 and 4 to calculate the cost per tube. Ifan alloy tube listed
in table 3 is used, multiply the quantity from table 4 by the factor in
table 3. :rubes not shown will not require the TOOLING part.

SUbject: RE: Zinc metallize weights per tube
New rule for zinc metalized tUbe ends: For jobs that require zinc metalized tUbe ends, Production Engineering (Steve and
Jonathan) will add the quantity of zinc to the 6A-4 EBOM when the skeleton BaM is first created, same as has been done
to date. The quantity of zinc will be 0.045 Ibs per tube, regardless of tube diameter. This supercedes the old rule of 0.025
Ibs per tube per inch of diameter, which superceded 0.09 Ibs per tube per inch of diameter.
This will need to be updated in our standards books.

5.13 HOOO-6X
5.13.1 Components include:
I HOOO-6X-z
Header plate
Cover plates
Model W603 Name Plate Bracket
Model W601 Header Shipping Lug
Welding Materials
ETa name plate brackets (unless made from header material)
ETa lifting lugs (unless made from header material)
Other plate welded to header box
5.13.2 Header plate is separated and grouped by plate size for all boxes in a bundle.
Individual pieces (tube sheet, end plate, etc.) are not listed separately.
5.13.2.1 When plate material is stocked, use the part number for the 96x336
plate size. The unit ofmeasure is "EA". Show quantities as a decimal
fraction of full plates required.
5.13.2.2 When plate material is not stocked, use a part number for the material
and thickness ofplaterequired. Theunit ofmeasure ofthese partswill
be "SF". This is commonly referred to as "random" plate.
5.13.2.3 Header drawings created with Pro Engineer will not show plate
grouped as mentioned above. These bills will follow a similar format
as other drawings. Details will follow in a later release ofthis
document.

STD BOOK SECT. 3C -PC. 6
3.1 0 Retube Projects
3.10.1 Drawing Part Number is D#OOO-RT
3.1 0.2 Part Number Scope
a. Creation ofall forms related to the retubing of all process bundles on a given
project, including any and all revisions to those forms.
b. This part number covers the retube scope ofwork only.
c. If a retube project includes other scope such as machinery mounts, part numbers
will be created to represent that work.
3.11 Proposal Projects
3.11.1 No part number is created for this type of project. Charge time to transaction ~.
3.11.2 Project Scope
Create miscellaneous drawings and/or drive selections for a given project
3.12 Sales Order Proj ects
3.12.1 No part number is created for this type of project. Charge time directly to the sales
order number.
3.12.2 Project Scope
Create miscellaneous drawings for a given project.
3.12.3 Steps for charging direct labor to sales order:
a. Log onto Visibility; enter TA for Selection: from the main menu; then enter 07,
to advance onto the Manual Assignment screen.
b. Enter the department and transaction type in Dept: __, Trans Type: SO .
c. Enter the sales order number for Charge No: __ . Use the Enter key to
advance to the employee number prompt.
d. Enter Employee No., Labor Opn/Code, and Clock-In time.
e. Update information (US or UR)
3.13 Header BOM, Miscellaneous Work, and Revisions
3.13.1 Part Number is D#OOO-JOB
3.13.2 Part Number Scope
a. Administrative work performed by drafting supervisors.
b. Revisions that occur after a drawing has been issued.
c. Miscellaneous project work by structural and header design engineers.
d. Miscellaneous project work (refer to table 3).

3.14 Finite Element Analysis (FEA)
3.14.1 A part number is created in the form ofD#OOO-FEAX; where X equals the
drawings, for example, 6A (FEAA), 6B (FEAB), and so on.
3.14.2 The steps required to complete the FEA are covered in the scope for the header
design part numbers (D#000-H6X) and D#OOO-JOB.
3.14.3 Refer to section 10 (Operation Scope of Work) of this document for instructions on
which steps go with which part numbers.
3.15 Other part numbers and/or routing operations will be created for engineering activities on a
case-by-case basis (determined by Production Engineering and the Drafting Manager) when a
situation does not fit the standard. The following are some examples of when this would
occur.
a. Non-ACHE jobs such as the Split-Flo® and various Therm-Flo® products.
b. ACHE projects with unusual requirements.
3.16 The Parts Master Administrator (PMA) should use the following default values for each
drawing part number.
3.16.1 Part Master Maintenance parameters:
a. MakelBuy Code = M
b. Planner Code = 30
c. Unit ofMeasure = DW
d. Commodity Code = EDET
